- [Soft But Royal](https://librasluxury.com/products/soft-but-royal): Soft But RoyalThere's a difference between being loud and being heard. Between demanding attention and naturally commanding it. This tee understands that difference.Soft But Royal isn't a contradictionit's a philosophy. It's the understanding that true power doesn't need to announce itself. That luxury whispers while trends shout. That you can move through the world with grace and still leave an unforgettable impression.This is for the ones who know their worth without needing validation. The ones who carry themselves with quiet confidence and let their presence do the talking. The ones who understand that being soft doesn't mean being weakit means being strong enough to stay grounded while still standing out.The LibrasLuxury DifferenceEvery piece we create is designed with intention. Soft But Royal embodies our commitment to balanceblending premium comfort with elevated style, modern streetwear energy with timeless sophistication. This isn't fast fashion. This is a piece that becomes part of your identity, your daily uniform, your signature look.Crafted from premium cotton that feels like luxury against your skin, this tee is built to move with you through every momentfrom morning coffee runs to late-night creative sessions, from casual meetups to making power moves. It's effortlessly versatile because your life doesn't fit into one box, and neither should your wardrobe.Why You'll Love It Luxurious Comfort That Lasts - Premium 5.3 oz. cotton crafted from sustainably and fairly grown USA cotton. This isn't just softit's the kind of quality you feel the moment you put it on and every time after. Built With Intention - Double-needle stitching throughout, reinforced shoulder-to-shoulder taping, and a seamless rib collar mean this piece is designed to withstand your lifestyle while maintaining its royal status wash after wash. The Perfect Fit, Every Time - Classic fit with quarter-turned construction eliminates center creasing. 100% preshrunk cotton means it fits right from day one and stays true to sizeno surprises, just consistency. Effortlessly Elevated - Dress it up with tailored pieces or keep it street with your favorite joggers. Layer it under a blazer or let it stand alone. This tee adapts to your energy while keeping that LibrasLuxury edge intact. Thoughtful Details - From the tear-away label for maximum comfort to the carefully selected fabric blend, every detail is intentional. Because luxury is in the details you don't see but definitely feel. The Specs 5.3 oz., 100% preshrunk cotton (select heather colors are cotton/poly blends for enhanced texture) Made with sustainably and fairly grown USA cottonluxury with a conscience Seamless 7/8" rib collar that holds its shape Taped shoulder-to-shoulder for lasting durability Double-needle stitching on sleeves and bottom hem Tear away labelno distractions, just comfort Classic fit designed to flatter without being restrictive Quarter-turned to eliminate center crease The MovementSoft But Royal represents more than a productit's a mindset. It's for those who build different, move with purpose, and understand that true luxury isn't about logos or hype. It's about knowing who you are and moving like it.This is your daily reminder that you don't need to be the loudest in the room to be the most powerful. That grace and strength can coexist. That you can be soft in your approach and still royal in your outcome.Silent Strength. Quiet Power. Golden Outcome.Welcome to LibrasLuxurywhere quiet confidence meets golden power.
